JSON Canvas Specification for Obsidian","","Version 1.0 — 2024-03-11","","## Overview","","JSON Canvas is a format for representing infinite canvas documents. This specification defines the structure for creating canvas files compatible with Obsidian.","","## Top Level Structure","","The root JSON object contains two optional arrays:","","```json","{","  \"nodes\": [...],","  \"edges\": [...]","}","```","","- `nodes` (optional, array): All canvas objects (text, files, links, groups)","- `edges` (optional, array): All connections between nodes","","## Node Types","","### Common Attributes","","All nodes share these required attributes:","","- `id` (required, string): Unique identifier for the node","- `type` (required, string): Node type (`text`, `file`, `link`, `group`)","- `x` (required, integer): X position in pixels","- `y` (required, integer): Y position in pixels","- `width` (required, integer): Width in pixels","- `height` (required, integer): Height in pixels","- `color` (optional, string/number): Color (hex `\"#FF0000\"` or preset `\"1\"`)","","### Text Nodes","","Store plain text with Markdown formatting.","","**Required Attributes:**","- `text` (string): Content in Markdown syntax","","**Example:**","```json","{","  \"id\": \"abc123\",","  \"type\": \"text\",","  \"x\": 0,","  \"y\": 0,","  \"width\": 250,","  \"height\": 100,","  \"text\": \"# Main Topic\\n\\nKey point here\",","  \"color\": \"4\"","}","```","","### File Nodes","","Reference other files or attachments (images, PDFs, etc.).","","**Required Attributes:**","- `file` (string): Path to file in the vault","","**Optional Attributes:**","- `subpath` (string): Link to specific heading/block (starts with `#`)","","**Example:**","```json","{","  \"id\": \"def456\",","  \"type\": \"file\",","  \"x\": 300,","  \"y\": 0,","  \"width\": 400,","  \"height\": 300,","  \"file\": \"Images/diagram.png\"","}","```","","**With Subpath:**","```json","{","  \"id\": \"ghi789\",","  \"type\": \"file\",","  \"x\": 0,","  \"y\": 200,","  \"width\": 250,","  \"height\": 100,","  \"file\": \"Notes/Meeting Notes.md\",","  \"subpath\": \"#Action Items\"","}","```","","### Link Nodes","","Reference external URLs.","","**Required Attributes:**","- `url` (string): Full URL including protocol","","**Example:**","```json","{","  \"id\": \"jkl012\",","  \"type\": \"link\",","  \"x\": 0,","  \"y\": -200,","  \"width\": 250,","  \"height\": 100,","  \"url\": \"https://obsidian.md\",","  \"color\": \"5\"","}","```","","### Group Nodes","","Visual containers for organizing related nodes.","","**Optional Attributes:**","- `label` (string): Text label for the group (recommended)","- `background` (string): Path to background image","- `backgroundStyle` (string): Image rendering style","  - `cover`: Fill entire node","  - `ratio`: Maintain aspect ratio","  - `repeat`: Tile as pattern","","**Example:**","```json","{","  \"id\": \"group1\",","  \"type\": \"group\",","  \"x\": -50,","  \"y\": -50,","  \"width\": 600,","  \"height\": 400,","  \"label\": \"Main Concepts\",","  \"color\": \"4\"","}","```","","**With Background:**","```json","{","  \"id\": \"group2\",","  \"type\": \"group\",","  \"x\": 700,","  \"y\": 0,","  \"width\": 500,","  \"height\": 600,","  \"label\": \"Reference Materials\",","  \"background\": \"Images/texture.png\",","  \"backgroundStyle\": \"repeat\"","}","```","","## Z-Index and Layering","","Nodes are displayed in array order:","- **First node**: Bottom layer (rendered below others)","- **Last node**: Top layer (rendered above others)","","**Best Practice Order:**","1. Group nodes (backgrounds)","2. Sub-groups","3. Regular nodes (text, file, link)","","This ensures groups appear behind content.","","## Edges (Connections)","","Edges connect nodes with lines.","","**Required Attributes:**","- `id` (required, string): Unique identifier","- `fromNode` (required, string): Starting node ID","- `toNode` (required, string): Ending node ID","","**Optional Attributes:**","- `fromSide` (string): Starting edge side","  - Values: `top`, `right`, `bottom`, `left`","- `fromEnd` (string): Start endpoint shape","  - Values: `none` (default), `arrow`","- `toSide` (string): Ending edge side","  - Values: `top`, `right`, `bottom`, `left`","- `toEnd` (string): End endpoint shape","  - Values: `arrow` (default), `none`","- `color` (string/number): Edge color","- `label` (string): Text label on edge","","**Example - Simple Connection:**","```json","{","  \"id\": \"edge1\",","  \"fromNode\": \"abc123\",","  \"toNode\": \"def456\"","}","```","","**Example - Fully Specified:**","```json","{","  \"id\": \"edge2\",","  \"fromNode\": \"def456\",","  \"fromSide\": \"bottom\",","  \"fromEnd\": \"none\",","  \"toNode\": \"ghi789\",","  \"toSide\": \"top\",","  \"toEnd\": \"arrow\",","  \"color\": \"3\",","  \"label\": \"leads to\"","}","```","","## Color System","","### Preset Colors","","Use string numbers `\"1\"` through `\"6\"`:","","- `\"1\"` - Red","- `\"2\"` - Orange","- `\"3\"` - Yellow","- `\"4\"` - Green","- `\"5\"` - Cyan","- `\"6\"` - Purple","","**Note:** Exact colors adapt to Obsidian's theme. These provide semantic meaning across light/dark modes.","","### Custom Hex Colors","","Use hex format: `\"#RRGGBB\"`","","**Examples:**","- `\"#4A90E2\"` (blue)","- `\"#50E3C2\"` (teal)","- `\"#F5A623\"` (orange)","","**Best Practice:** Use consistent format within a canvas (all hex OR all presets).","","## Complete Example","","```json","{","  \"nodes\": [","    {","      \"id\": \"group001\",","      \"type\": \"group\",","      \"x\": -50,","      \"y\": -50,","      \"width\": 700,","      \"height\": 500,","      \"label\": \"Core Concepts\",","      \"color\": \"4\"","    },","    {","      \"id\": \"center01\",","      \"type\": \"text\",","      \"x\": 0,","      \"y\": 0,","      \"width\": 300,","      \"height\": 120,","      \"text\": \"# Central Topic\\n\\nMain idea here\",","      \"color\": \"4\"","    },","    {","      \"id\": \"branch01\",","      \"type\": \"text\",","      \"x\": 400,","      \"y\": -100,","      \"width\": 220,","      \"height\": 100,","      \"text\": \"Subtopic A\",","      \"color\": \"5\"","    },","    {","      \"id\": \"branch02\",","      \"type\": \"text\",","      \"x\": 400,","      \"y\": 100,","      \"width\": 220,","      \"height\": 100,","      \"text\": \"Subtopic B\",","      \"color\": \"5\"","    },","    {","      \"id\": \"detail01\",","      \"type\": \"text\",","      \"x\": 700,","      \"y\": -100,","      \"width\": 200,","      \"height\": 80,","      \"text\": \"Detail 1\",","      \"color\": \"6\"","    }","  ],","  \"edges\": [","    {","      \"id\": \"e1\",","      \"fromNode\": \"center01\",","      \"fromSide\": \"right\",","      \"toNode\": \"branch01\",","      \"toSide\": \"left\",","      \"toEnd\": \"arrow\"","    },","    {","      \"id\": \"e2\",","      \"fromNode\": \"center01\",","      \"fromSide\": \"right\",","      \"toNode\": \"branch02\",","      \"toSide\": \"left\",","      \"toEnd\": \"arrow\"","    },","    {","      \"id\": \"e3\",","      \"fromNode\": \"branch01\",","      \"fromSide\": \"right\",","      \"toNode\": \"detail01\",","      \"toSide\": \"left\",","      \"toEnd\": \"arrow\",","      \"color\": \"3\"","    }","  ]","}","```","","## Validation Requirements","","When creating canvas files, ensure:","","1. **Unique IDs**: All `id` values must be unique across nodes and edges","2. **Valid References**: All edge `fromNode` and `toNode` must reference existing node IDs","3. **Required Fields**: All required attributes are present for each type","4. **Valid Coordinates**: All position/dimension values are integers","5. **Color Format**: Colors use either hex (`\"#RRGGBB\"`) or preset strings (`\"1\"` to `\"6\"`)","6. **Quote Escaping**: Special characters properly escaped in JSON strings","","## Common Issues and Solutions","","### Issue: Canvas won't open in Obsidian","**Solutions:**","- Validate JSON syntax (use JSON validator)","- Check all IDs are unique","- Verify all edge references exist","- Ensure required fields present","","### Issue: Nodes appear overlapped","**Solutions:**","- Increase spacing between coordinates","- Account for node dimensions in positioning","- Use minimum spacing: 320px horizontal, 200px vertical","","### Issue: Groups don't show properly","**Solutions:**","- Ensure groups appear before content nodes in array","- Add explicit `label` to all groups","- Check group dimensions encompass child nodes","","### Issue: Colors don't match expectations","**Solutions:**","- Use consistent color format (all hex OR all presets)","- Remember presets adapt to theme","- Test in both light and dark mode if using custom colors","","### Issue: Text appears truncated","**Solutions:**","- Increase node dimensions","- Break long text into multiple nodes","- Use file nodes for lengthy content","","## Character Encoding for Chinese Content","","When canvas contains Chinese text, apply these transformations:","","- Chinese double quotes `\"` → `『』`","- Chinese single quotes `'` → `「」`","- English double quotes must be escaped: `\\\"`","","**Example:**","```json","{","  \"text\": \"『核心概念』包含:「子概念A」和「子概念B」\"","}","```","","This prevents JSON parsing errors with mixed-language content.","","## Performance Considerations","","- **Large Canvases**: Keep node count reasonable (\u003c500 for smooth performance)","- **Image Files**: Use compressed images for backgrounds","- **Text Length**: Keep node text concise; use file nodes for long content","- **Edge Complexity**: Minimize crossing edges for clarity","","## Future Extensions","","This specification may be extended with:","- Additional node types","- More edge styling options","- Animation properties","- Interactive behaviors","","Always check Obsidian documentation for latest Canvas features."],"stylingDirectives":null,"colorizedLines":["\u003cspan class=\"pl-mh\"\u003e# \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eJSON Canvas Specification for Obsidian\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e","","Version 1.0 — 2024-03-11","","\u003cspan class=\"pl-mh\"\u003e## \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eOverview\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e","","JSON Canvas is a format for representing infinite canvas documents. This specification defines the structure for creating canvas files compatible with Obsidian.","","\u003cspan class=\"pl-mh\"\u003e## \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eTop Level Structure\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e","","The root JSON object contains two optional arrays:","","\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e```\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003ejson\u003c/span\u003e","{","  \u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003e\u0026quot;nodes\u0026quot;\u003c/span\u003e: [\u003cspan class=\"pl-ii\"\u003e...\u003c/span\u003e],","  \u003cspan (optional, array): All canvas objects (text, files, links, groups)","\u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003e-\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003eedges\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e (optional, array): All connections between nodes","","\u003cspan class=\"pl-mh\"\u003e## \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eNode Types\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e","","\u003cspan class=\"pl-mh\"\u003e### \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eCommon Attributes\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e","","All class=\"pl-s\"\u003e```\u003c/span\u003e","","\u003cspan class=\"pl-mh\"\u003e### \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eLink Nodes\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e","","Reference external URLs.","","\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003eRequired Attributes:\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003e-\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003eurl\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e (string): Full URL including protocol","","\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003eExample:\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e```\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003ejson\u003c/span\u003e","{","  \u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003e\u0026quot;id\u0026quot;\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\u0026quot;\u003c/span\u003ejkl012\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\u0026quot;\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e,","  \u003cspan class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">JSON Canvas Specification for Obsidian</h1><a id="user-content-json-canvas-specification-for-obsidian" <p dir="auto">Version 1.0 — 2024-03-11</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Overview</h2><a id="user-content-overview" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Overview" href="#overview"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">JSON Canvas is a format for representing infinite canvas documents. This specification defines the structure for creating canvas files compatible with Obsidian.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Top Level Structure</h2><a id="user-content-top-level-structure" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Top Level Structure" href="#top-level-structure"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The root JSON object contains two optional arrays:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;nodes&quot;: [...],
  &quot;edges&quot;: [...]
}"><pre>{
  <span class="pl-ent">"nodes"</span>: [<span class="pl-ii">...</span>],
  <span class="pl-ent">"edges"</span>: [<span class="pl-ii">...</span>]
}</pre></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>nodes</code> (optional, array): All canvas objects (text, files, links, groups)</li>
<li><code>edges</code> (optional, array): All connections between nodes</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Node Types</h2><a id="user-content-node-types" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Node Types" href="#node-types"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Common Attributes</h3><a id="user-content-common-attributes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Common Attributes" href="#common-attributes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">All nodes share these required attributes:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>id</code> (required, string): Unique identifier for the node</li>
<li><code>type</code> (required, string): Node type (<code>text</code>, <code>file</code>, <code>link</code>, <code>group</code>)</li>
<li><code>x</code> (required, integer): X position in pixels</li>
<li><code>y</code> (required, integer): Y position in pixels</li>
<li><code>width</code> (required, integer): Width in pixels</li>
<li><code>height</code> (required, integer): Height in pixels</li>
<li><code>color</code> (optional, string/number): Color (hex <code>"#FF0000"</code> or preset <code>"1"</code>)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Text Nodes</h3><a id="user-content-text-nodes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Text Nodes" href="#text-nodes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Store plain text with Markdown formatting.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Required Attributes:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>text</code> (string): Content in Markdown syntax</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Example:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;id&quot;: &quot;abc123&quot;,
  &quot;type&quot;: &quot;text&quot;,
  &quot;x&quot;: 0,
  &quot;y&quot;: 0,
  &quot;width&quot;: 250,
  &quot;height&quot;: 100,
  &quot;text&quot;: &quot;# Main Topic\n\nKey point here&quot;,
  &quot;color&quot;: &quot;4&quot;
}"><pre>{
  <span class="pl-ent">"id"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>abc123<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>text<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"x"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">0</span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"y"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">0</span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"width"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">250</span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"height"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">100</span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"text"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span># Main Topic<span class="pl-cce">\n\n</span>Key point here<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"color"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>4<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
}</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">File Nodes</h3><a id="user-content-file-nodes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: File Nodes" href="#file-nodes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Reference other files or attachments (images, PDFs, etc.).</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Required Attributes:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>file</code> (string): Path to file in the vault</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Optional Attributes:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>subpath</code> (string): Link to specific heading/block (starts with <code>#</code>)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Example:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;id&quot;: &quot;def456&quot;,
  &quot;type&quot;: &quot;file&quot;,
  &quot;x&quot;: 300,
  &quot;y&quot;: 0,
  &quot;width&quot;: 400,
  &quot;height&quot;: 300,
  &quot;file&quot;: &quot;Images/diagram.png&quot;
}"><pre>{
  <span class="pl-ent">"id"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>def456<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>file<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"x"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">300</span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"y"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">0</span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"width"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">400</span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"height"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">300</span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"file"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Images/diagram.png<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>With Subpath:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;id&quot;: &quot;ghi789&quot;,
  &quot;type&quot;: &quot;file&quot;,
  &quot;x&quot;: 0,
  &quot;y&quot;: 200,
  &quot;width&quot;: 250,
  &quot;height&quot;: 100,
  &quot;file&quot;: &quot;Notes/Meeting Notes.md&quot;,
  &quot;subpath&quot;: &quot;#Action Items&quot;
}"><pre>{
  <span class="pl-ent">"id"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>ghi789<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>file<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"x"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">0</span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"y"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">200</span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"width"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">250</span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"height"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">100</span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"file"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Notes/Meeting Notes.md<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"subpath"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>#Action Items<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
}</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Link Nodes</h3><a id="user-content-link-nodes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Link Nodes" href="#link-nodes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Reference external URLs.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Required Attributes:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>url</code> (string): Full URL including protocol</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Example:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;id&quot;: &quot;jkl012&quot;,
  &quot;type&quot;: &quot;link&quot;,
  &quot;x&quot;: 0,
  &quot;y&quot;: -200,
  &quot;width&quot;: 250,
  &quot;height&quot;: 100,
  &quot;url&quot;: &quot;https://obsidian.md&quot;,
  &quot;color&quot;: &quot;5&quot;
}"><pre>{
  <span class="pl-ent">"id"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>jkl012<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>link<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"x"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">0</span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"y"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">-200</span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"width"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">250</span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"height"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">100</span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"url"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>https://obsidian.md<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"color"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>5<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
}</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Group Nodes</h3><a id="user-content-group-nodes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Group Nodes" href="#group-nodes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Visual containers for organizing related nodes.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Optional Attributes:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>label</code> (string): Text label for the group (recommended)</li>
<li><code>background</code> (string): Path to background image</li>
<li><code>backgroundStyle</code> (string): Image rendering style
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>cover</code>: Fill entire node</li>
<li><code>ratio</code>: Maintain aspect ratio</li>
<li><code>repeat</code>: Tile as pattern</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Example:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;id&quot;: &quot;group1&quot;,
  &quot;type&quot;: &quot;group&quot;,
  &quot;x&quot;: -50,
  &quot;y&quot;: -50,
  &quot;width&quot;: 600,
  &quot;height&quot;: 400,
  &quot;label&quot;: &quot;Main Concepts&quot;,
  &quot;color&quot;: &quot;4&quot;
}"><pre>{
  <span class="pl-ent">"id"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>group1<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>group<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"x"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">-50</span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"y"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">-50</span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"width"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">600</span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"height"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">400</span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"label"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Main Concepts<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"color"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>4<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>With Background:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;id&quot;: &quot;group2&quot;,
  &quot;type&quot;: &quot;group&quot;,
  &quot;x&quot;: 700,
  &quot;y&quot;: 0,
  &quot;width&quot;: 500,
  &quot;height&quot;: 600,
  &quot;label&quot;: &quot;Reference Materials&quot;,
  &quot;background&quot;: &quot;Images/texture.png&quot;,
  &quot;backgroundStyle&quot;: &quot;repeat&quot;
}"><pre>{
  <span class="pl-ent">"id"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>group2<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"type"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>group<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"x"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">700</span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"y"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">0</span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"width"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">500</span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"height"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">600</span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"label"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Reference Materials<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"background"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Images/texture.png<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"backgroundStyle"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>repeat<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
}</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Z-Index and Layering</h2><a id="user-content-z-index-and-layering" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Z-Index and Layering" href="#z-index-and-layering"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Nodes are displayed in array order:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>First node</strong>: Bottom layer (rendered below others)</li>
<li><strong>Last node</strong>: Top layer (rendered above others)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Best Practice Order:</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Group nodes (backgrounds)</li>
<li>Sub-groups</li>
<li>Regular nodes (text, file, link)</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">This ensures groups appear behind content.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Edges (Connections)</h2><a id="user-content-edges-connections" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Edges (Connections)" href="#edges-connections"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Edges connect nodes with lines.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Required Attributes:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>id</code> (required, string): Unique identifier</li>
<li><code>fromNode</code> (required, string): Starting node ID</li>
<li><code>toNode</code> (required, string): Ending node ID</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Optional Attributes:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>fromSide</code> (string): Starting edge side
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Values: <code>top</code>, <code>right</code>, <code>bottom</code>, <code>left</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>fromEnd</code> (string): Start endpoint shape
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Values: <code>none</code> (default), <code>arrow</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>toSide</code> (string): Ending edge side
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Values: <code>top</code>, <code>right</code>, <code>bottom</code>, <code>left</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>toEnd</code> (string): End endpoint shape
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Values: <code>arrow</code> (default), <code>none</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>color</code> (string/number): Edge color</li>
<li><code>label</code> (string): Text label on edge</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Example - Simple Connection:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;id&quot;: &quot;edge1&quot;,
  &quot;fromNode&quot;: &quot;abc123&quot;,
  &quot;toNode&quot;: &quot;def456&quot;
}"><pre>{
  <span class="pl-ent">"id"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>edge1<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"fromNode"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>abc123<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"toNode"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>def456<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Example - Fully Specified:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;id&quot;: &quot;edge2&quot;,
  &quot;fromNode&quot;: &quot;def456&quot;,
  &quot;fromSide&quot;: &quot;bottom&quot;,
  &quot;fromEnd&quot;: &quot;none&quot;,
  &quot;toNode&quot;: &quot;ghi789&quot;,
  &quot;toSide&quot;: &quot;top&quot;,
  &quot;toEnd&quot;: &quot;arrow&quot;,
  &quot;color&quot;: &quot;3&quot;,
  &quot;label&quot;: &quot;leads to&quot;
}"><pre>{
  <span class="pl-ent">"id"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>edge2<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"fromNode"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>def456<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"fromSide"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>bottom<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"fromEnd"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>none<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"toNode"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>ghi789<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"toSide"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>top<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"toEnd"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>arrow<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"color"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>3<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-ent">"label"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>leads to<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
}</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Color System</h2><a id="user-content-color-system" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Color System" href="#color-system"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Preset Colors</h3><a id="user-content-preset-colors" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Preset Colors" href="#preset-colors"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Use string numbers <code>"1"</code> through <code>"6"</code>:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>"1"</code> - Red</li>
<li><code>"2"</code> - Orange</li>
<li><code>"3"</code> - Yellow</li>
<li><code>"4"</code> - Green</li>
<li><code>"5"</code> - Cyan</li>
<li><code>"6"</code> - Purple</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Note:</strong> Exact colors adapt to Obsidian's theme. These provide semantic meaning across light/dark modes.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Custom Hex Colors</h3><a id="user-content-custom-hex-colors" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Custom Hex Colors" href="#custom-hex-colors"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Use hex format: <code>"#RRGGBB"</code></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Examples:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>"#4A90E2"</code> (blue)</li>
<li><code>"#50E3C2"</code> (teal)</li>
<li><code>"#F5A623"</code> (orange)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Best Practice:</strong> Use consistent format within a canvas (all hex OR all presets).</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Complete Example</h2><a id="user-content-complete-example" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Complete Example" href="#complete-example"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

  ]
}</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Validation Requirements</h2><a id="user-content-validation-requirements" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Validation Requirements" href="#validation-requirements"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">When creating canvas files, ensure:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Unique IDs</strong>: All <code>id</code> values must be unique across nodes and edges</li>
<li><strong>Valid References</strong>: All edge <code>fromNode</code> and <code>toNode</code> must reference existing node IDs</li>
<li><strong>Required Fields</strong>: All required attributes are present for each type</li>
<li><strong>Valid Coordinates</strong>: All position/dimension values are integers</li>
<li><strong>Color Format</strong>: Colors use either hex (<code>"#RRGGBB"</code>) or preset strings (<code>"1"</code> to <code>"6"</code>)</li>
<li><strong>Quote Escaping</strong>: Special characters properly escaped in JSON strings</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Common Issues and Solutions</h2><a id="user-content-common-issues-and-solutions" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Common Issues and Solutions" href="#common-issues-and-solutions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Issue: Canvas won't open in Obsidian</h3><a id="user-content-issue-canvas-wont-open-in-obsidian" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Issue: Canvas won't open in Obsidian" href="#issue-canvas-wont-open-in-obsidian"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Solutions:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Validate JSON syntax (use JSON validator)</li>
<li>Check all IDs are unique</li>
<li>Verify all edge references exist</li>
<li>Ensure required fields present</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Issue: Nodes appear overlapped</h3><a id="user-content-issue-nodes-appear-overlapped" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Issue: Nodes appear overlapped" href="#issue-nodes-appear-overlapped"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Solutions:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Increase spacing between coordinates</li>
<li>Account for node dimensions in positioning</li>
<li>Use minimum spacing: 320px horizontal, 200px vertical</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Issue: Groups don't show properly</h3><a id="user-content-issue-groups-dont-show-properly" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Issue: Groups don't show properly" href="#issue-groups-dont-show-properly"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Solutions:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Ensure groups appear before content nodes in array</li>
<li>Add explicit <code>label</code> to all groups</li>
<li>Check group dimensions encompass child nodes</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Issue: Colors don't match expectations</h3><a id="user-content-issue-colors-dont-match-expectations" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Issue: Colors don't match expectations" href="#issue-colors-dont-match-expectations"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Solutions:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Use consistent color format (all hex OR all presets)</li>
<li>Remember presets adapt to theme</li>
<li>Test in both light and dark mode if using custom colors</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Issue: Text appears truncated</h3><a id="user-content-issue-text-appears-truncated" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Issue: Text appears truncated" href="#issue-text-appears-truncated"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Solutions:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Increase node dimensions</li>
<li>Break long text into multiple nodes</li>
<li>Use file nodes for lengthy content</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Character Encoding for Chinese Content</h2><a id="user-content-character-encoding-for-chinese-content" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Character Encoding for Chinese Content" href="#character-encoding-for-chinese-content"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">When canvas contains Chinese text, apply these transformations:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Chinese double quotes <code>"</code> → <code>『』</code></li>
<li>Chinese single quotes <code>'</code> → <code>「」</code></li>
<li>English double quotes must be escaped: <code>\"</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Example:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;text&quot;: &quot;『核心概念』包含:「子概念A」和「子概念B」&quot;
}"><pre>{
  <span class="pl-ent">"text"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>『核心概念』包含:「子概念A」和「子概念B」<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">This prevents JSON parsing errors with mixed-language content.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Performance Considerations</h2><a id="user-content-performance-considerations" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Performance Considerations" href="#performance-considerations"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Large Canvases</strong>: Keep node count reasonable (&lt;500 for smooth performance)</li>
<li><strong>Image Files</strong>: Use compressed images for backgrounds</li>
<li><strong>Text Length</strong>: Keep node text concise; use file nodes for long content</li>
<li><strong>Edge Complexity</strong>: Minimize crossing edges for clarity</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Future Extensions</h2><a id="user-content-future-extensions" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Future Extensions" href="#future-extensions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This specification may be extended with:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Additional node types</li>
<li>More edge styling options</li>
<li>Animation properties</li>
<li>Interactive behaviors</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Always check Obsidian documentation for latest Canvas features.</p>
